  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5b46cc60-1e5b-4be1-ae7b-c197e4917108'

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer5186295786748894661">From the busy city life of Dublin, Ireland to the quiet little town of Hilton Head, South Carolina, two lives are pulled together by tragedy and something more--call it fate, call it faeries.<br/><br/>After giving up a daughter for adoption at sixteen, KATLYN REYNOLDS has built a successful advertising company to keep her mind busy and her heart safe. But this pain from her past has</span>
  <span id="freeText5186295786748894661" style="display:none">From the busy city life of Dublin, Ireland to the quiet little town of Hilton Head, South Carolina, two lives are pulled together by tragedy and something more--call it fate, call it faeries.<br /><br />After giving up a daughter for adoption at sixteen, KATLYN REYNOLDS has built a successful advertising company to keep her mind busy and her heart safe. But this pain from her past has made Kate a use 'em and leave 'em kind of girl, bypassing love and commitment to protect herself. And this system has worked--<br /><br />--until she meets DEACON O'MALLERY, a sweet, sexy, striving Irish businessman. Deacon is known as a jammy, a lucky bastard. As second in command at the largest intel company in Europe, he has the world by the balls, leaving the orphaned boy who grew up with nothing--and everyone else--behind. Then Katlyn Reynolds walks into his life and he's smitten. Kate is his maité Sol, his soul mate; he just knows it; even his wanker can't stop thinking about her. And, for the first time, after hearing Kate's story of brutality and loss, he wants to find his birth mother, the woman who abandoned him.<br /><br />Kate's feelings for Deacon are confusing. She cares enough to reveal her past, but insists he find love somewhere else.<br /><br />Now this stubborn bloke has two missions: to find his mother and to make the girl across the ocean stand by his side forever. Ádh mór ort, Kate! Good luck, he thinks. She's going to need it to fight him off, for he has more than good looks, charm, tenacity, and money on his side. Deacon has Thomas and Calista: spirits he unwittingly beckons into his life.<br /><br />In the second book in the Soul Mate series the cross-continental frolics continue with Kate and Deacon. Drama blends with desire and an off-the-charts plot, creating the heavyweight champion of page-turners in this sensual romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5186295786748894661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

<div id="review_1929324647" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1929324647" />
    <a title="Susan Hampson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36613708-susan-hampson"><img alt="Susan Hampson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573295524p2/36613708.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1929324647?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan Hampson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan Hampson" href="/user/show/36613708-susan-hampson">Susan Hampson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1929324647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9957356077443683923">Well be prepared to enter a world of fantasy involving mystical angels, romance and erotica all wrapped in a story that would touch anyone's heart. This is the second novel in the Soul Mates series and it flowed on beautifully from Your Soul was made for Mine. <br/>Katlyn Reynolds is a very confident  business woman from the United States that can hold her own in any boardroom but after forming an online relationship with Deacon O'Malley from Ireland, a major player in the largest Intel Company in Eu</span>
  <span id="freeText9957356077443683923" style="display:none">Well be prepared to enter a world of fantasy involving mystical angels, romance and erotica all wrapped in a story that would touch anyone's heart. This is the second novel in the Soul Mates series and it flowed on beautifully from Your Soul was made for Mine. <br />Katlyn Reynolds is a very confident  business woman from the United States that can hold her own in any boardroom but after forming an online relationship with Deacon O'Malley from Ireland, a major player in the largest Intel Company in Europe, she simply goes to pieces in his presence. In this book Kate sneaks into Ireland to see her friends Emmalyn and Nolan but it isn't long before Deacon crosses her path. The chemistry is too much to stay away from each other but Deacon is in for a bit of a shock. This isn't the Kate he thought he knew. They both have secrets from their pasts. <br />Deacon finally believes in the existence of the angels Thomas and Calista,  and I was enthralled with the story behind why humans have the dent between their nose and mouth. It is just charming. It is one of those stories that will always stick with you. <br />C. L. Hunter has created a brilliant story line around Kate and Deacon that just left me  emotionally spent. They both need to face their demons and hunt down their pasts but not everything is so cut and dried. Once you know something then it can't be unknown. I am still on a high from reading this book. I loved the first book but this one is definitely the heart and soul. So looking forward to the third book coming out soon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9957356077443683923" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1929038331" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12811848037898593195">My Soul Belongs To You<br/>CL Hunter<br/>4 stars<br/><br/>This is the second book in the Soul Mate series. I read this book back to back with the first release. Although these books are standalones I was really happy to read them right after each other. The two characters in this book you do meet in the first however not reading them in order will not hinder your enjoyment. <br/><br/>Deacon and Kate -- another romance across the countryside. Deacon is successful -- Kate is sassy and confident. Both are a catch but both have </span>
  <span id="freeText12811848037898593195" style="display:none">My Soul Belongs To You<br />CL Hunter<br />4 stars<br /><br />This is the second book in the Soul Mate series. I read this book back to back with the first release. Although these books are standalones I was really happy to read them right after each other. The two characters in this book you do meet in the first however not reading them in order will not hinder your enjoyment. <br /><br />Deacon and Kate -- another romance across the countryside. Deacon is successful -- Kate is sassy and confident. Both are a catch but both have a past. Kate has a past that defines her confidence although she is successful and doesn't allow her to trust much anyone. Deacon has no issues attracting women and isn't fond of keeping a relationship on his calendar. <br /><br />During a video conference these two see something in the other they like. However small moments cannot pave the way over the rough heart and ideas that lie in Kates head. Rocky roads make it almost seem impossible to continue trying and with Deacon's life being threatened along the way it seems as if nothing is going to work to try and shine light on either of them. <br /><br />I really loved the "interventions" that came into play in order to give Deacon and Kate hope. Again this was not my normal read but I loved the way the characters were written and my heart was hurt over their hardships. Click this release up as well as the previous. Its well worth your time. Thank you for the chance to read -- Review to post to Ramblings From Beneath The Sheets. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15508951444219339814">My Soul Belongs to You by CL Hunter is a true love story about what it really means to love someone completely and unselfishly. It is full of twists and turns and surprises. This book is part of a series, the second book - the first being Your Soul was made for Mine.   <span id="freeText15508951444219339814" style="display:none">My Soul Belongs to You by CL Hunter is a true love story about what it really means to love someone completely and unselfishly. It is full of twists and turns and surprises. This book is part of a series, the second book - the first being Your Soul was made for Mine. It is a fast moving read, never boring and it is easy to get attached to the characters. My Soul Belongs to You has a uniqueness to the plot and is a very good read. Sometimes it is a little steamy, but still realistic and not vulgar. Recommended reading for romance lovers.</span>

<div id="review_1908893768" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1908893768" />
    <a title="Reader Views" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48888810-reader-views"><img alt="Reader Views" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600777637p2/48888810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1908893768?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reader Views" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reader Views" href="/user/show/48888810-reader-views">Reader Views</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1908893768" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10745245387679854063">Reviewed by Sheri Hoyte for Reader Views (02/17)<br/><br/>Article first published as <a href='http://blogcritics.org/book-review-my-soul-belongs-to-you-by-c-l-hunter' rel='nofollow noopener'>Book Review: ‘My Soul Belongs to You’ by C.L. Hunter on Blogcritics</a><a></a>.<br/><br/>“My Soul Belongs to You” is the second book in the Soul Mates series by C.L. Hunter. Merging the magical and mystical delights of a fantasy novel, the suspenseful anticipation of a great mystery/thriller, and the intimate interludes of a steamy romance; it is a story full of enticement, page after enchanting page.<br/><br/>As the owner of a successful advertising a</span>
  <span id="freeText10745245387679854063" style="display:none">Reviewed by Sheri Hoyte for Reader Views (02/17)<br /><br />Article first published as <a href="http://blogcritics.org/book-review-my-soul-belongs-to-you-by-c-l-hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Review: ‘My Soul Belongs to You’ by C.L. Hunter on Blogcritics</a><a></a>.<br /><br />“My Soul Belongs to You” is the second book in the Soul Mates series by C.L. Hunter. Merging the magical and mystical delights of a fantasy novel, the suspenseful anticipation of a great mystery/thriller, and the intimate interludes of a steamy romance; it is a story full of enticement, page after enchanting page.<br /><br />As the owner of a successful advertising agency, Katlyn Reynolds is a powerful, career-driven, modern woman. Trading in love and commitment for authority and control, the walls Katlyn built do a great job of protecting her from life, and the pain of her past.<br /><br />Starved, abused, and orphaned as a young boy, Deacon O’Mallery rises above his inner turmoil to become second in command of the largest Intel company in Europe, shutting out the demons of old by focusing on business.<br /><br />When the two meet, there are undeniable sparks, but they will each have to overcome old ghosts and unexpected adversity if they are to have any hopes of a future together.<br /><br />Where to start? I absolutely loved this book! The writing is brilliant. The author is genuinely accomplished in her storytelling craft. It is clear a lot of research went into writing an authentic tale. As much of the book is set in Ireland, Hunter speaks clearly to readers of the traditions, and language of the Irish people, and the settings are described in such rich detail, one can easily imagine being right there in the beautiful countryside.<br /><br />There is so much going on in the story I really need to highlight some of the different elements. The suspenseful aspects in the plot take several unanticipated turns, catching me so off guard and causing me to stop reading and say aloud, “well done!” The fantasy components add just the right amount of magical aura, nudging the reader to delve deeper into their own beliefs. Then there’s the romantic spin – OH MY– breathtaking, exquisitely sexy, and stimulating–WOW factor all the way!<br /><br />The characters are well developed, relatable and grow with the story. They drive and pace the plot with their unique and captivating personalities. Readers will feel the emotional ups and downs, struggles, and triumphs of the characters, as if going through the experiences directly.<br /><br />Overall, I found “My Soul Belongs to You” by C.L. Hunter to be an excellent, well-rounded, entertaining read. Even though it is book two in the series, it does well as a standalone story–but the series is so well done, I highly recommend readers pick up Hunter’s first book, “Your Soul Was Made for Mine,” and read them in order for the full experience.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10745245387679854063" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1911594313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12086697090367259233">My Soul Belongs to you is the sequel to Your soul was made for mine by C.L Hunter. It is the 2nd book of the Soul Mates Series.<br/><br/>I received a copy from the author in turn for my honest review.<br/><br/>I Highly suggest you read the first book before this as there are several references to the previous book even though this book focuses on another couple.<br/><br/>5/5<br/><br/>In the second book in the Soul Mate series the cross-continental frolics continue with Kate and Deacon. Drama blends with desire and an off-the-charts pl</span>
  <span id="freeText12086697090367259233" style="display:none">My Soul Belongs to you is the sequel to Your soul was made for mine by C.L Hunter. It is the 2nd book of the Soul Mates Series.<br><br>I received a copy from the author in turn for my honest review.<br><br>I Highly suggest you read the first book before this as there are several references to the previous book even though this book focuses on another couple.<br><br>5/5<br><br>In the second book in the Soul Mate series the cross-continental frolics continue with Kate and Deacon. Drama blends with desire and an off-the-charts plot, creating the heavyweight champion of page-turners in this sensual romance.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>My soul belongs to you is an impressive book. The characters are expertly written and developed throughout the book - it's not hard to imagine them as real people as real as you and me.<br><br>Having read and reviewed the first book of the series I already knew Deacon &amp; Kate to some degree. However, their characters have developed a lot through this story - I personally believe Kate was an almost entirely different person by the end. Of course, I only say almost because come on it's Kate she's not one to back down without a challenge.<br><br>Be prepared for a story that will keep you on the edge of your seat. I personally feel this story wasn't as traditionally 'romantic' as the last. that, however, doesn't mean it wasn't worth reading - in fact, this story was blazing with heated passion, drama and 'action' from start to finish.<br><br>I don't know if this was intentional but I believe that the way this story is written reflects the personalities of Deacon and Kate and as they develop so does the atmosphere i.e. as the written becomes a little more romantic so do they. I love how this contrasts to the first book where it was like an amazing mosh pit of dreamy romance because that's who Emmalyn and Noel are they are a Dreamy Romantic mosh pit.<br><br>I 100% recommend not only this book but this series to any true romantmaniac like myself. It's full of magic, culture, heart-stopping relationships! ( and if that's not enough for you the 18+ scenes are greatly written and are honestly true 18+ XD )<br><br>Please Leave a comment with any questions/ thoughts.<br>you can also find the Author on Twitter as @Toughii2<br><br>Enjoy!!<br>Lesley<br>Creator &amp; CEO<br>Honestly Simple Reviews</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1846534992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8718736193885102470">This second book in the "Soul Mate Series" revolves around a couple from the previous novel. <br/><br/>Deacon is single. He lives in Ireland where he is part of a successful and renowned business. He has had his fair share of playing the field without commitments. <br/><br/>Kate is a confident business woman who has confidence and trust issues in her personal life. As a result of childhood and teenage traumas, she has to be in control of all aspects of her life. <br/><br/>Kate and Deacon met via a video conference and have b</span>
  <span id="freeText8718736193885102470" style="display:none">This second book in the "Soul Mate Series" revolves around a couple from the previous novel. <br /><br />Deacon is single. He lives in Ireland where he is part of a successful and renowned business. He has had his fair share of playing the field without commitments. <br /><br />Kate is a confident business woman who has confidence and trust issues in her personal life. As a result of childhood and teenage traumas, she has to be in control of all aspects of her life. <br /><br />Kate and Deacon met via a video conference and have been smitten with each other since. They had a brief encounter at their friends' wedding but decided not to take things any further despite the obvious attraction. <br /><br />Kate pays a visit to her friends in Ireland without Deacon's knowledge. Inadvertently, they come face to face which forces them to address some of their apprehensions about long term relationships. They are both tortured souls who have been through a lot of pain in the past. Deacon is quite prepared to take a chance whilst Kate doesn't think that she is "worthy" after everything that's happened to her. <br /><br />Kate eventually decides to have a go at a relationship with Deacon and when it looks like it might just work out, they face one obstacle after another. Deacon's life is being threatened. The lights that are shed on their pasts bring some shocking and impossible news. Is this relationship doomed? <br /><br />This novel has a paranormal twist with angelic interventions. The locations are descriptive enough to give the reader a realistic picture without interfering with the flow of the story. This could be a matter of preference! The romance is very poignant. Friends' loyalty and support are very well portrayed. The sex scenes are very graphic. The storyline is very well developed and full of suspense and surprises. <br /><br />This would appeal to those who like erotic novels with palpable emotions and endless twists.</span>

<div id="review_1861678788" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1861678788" />
    <a title="Brigitte " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34807917-brigitte"><img alt="Brigitte " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604558413p2/34807917.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1861678788?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brigitte " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brigitte " href="/user/show/34807917-brigitte">Brigitte </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/31334093-my-soul-belongs-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34807917-brigitte?shelf=2017">2017</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1861678788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3107263409163479288">This second book in the "Soul Mate Series" revolves around a couple from the previous novel. <br/><br/>Deacon is single. He lives in Ireland where he is part of a successful and renowned business. He has had his fair share of playing the field without commitments. <br/><br/>Kate is a confident business woman who has confidence and trust issues in her personal life. As a result of childhood and teenage traumas, she has to be in control of all aspects of her life. <br/><br/>Kate and Deacon met via a video conference and have b</span>
  <span id="freeText3107263409163479288" style="display:none">This second book in the "Soul Mate Series" revolves around a couple from the previous novel. <br /><br />Deacon is single. He lives in Ireland where he is part of a successful and renowned business. He has had his fair share of playing the field without commitments. <br /><br />Kate is a confident business woman who has confidence and trust issues in her personal life. As a result of childhood and teenage traumas, she has to be in control of all aspects of her life. <br /><br />Kate and Deacon met via a video conference and have been smitten with each other since. They had a brief encounter at their friends' wedding but decided not to take things any further despite the obvious attraction. <br /><br />Kate pays a visit to her friends in Ireland without Deacon's knowledge. Inadvertently, they come face to face which forces them to address some of their apprehensions about long term relationships. They are both tortured souls who have been through a lot of pain in the past. Deacon is quite prepared to take a chance whilst Kate doesn't think that she is "worthy" after everything that's happened to her. <br /><br />Kate eventually decides to have a go at a relationship with Deacon and when it looks like it might just work out, they face one obstacle after another. Deacon's life is being threatened. The lights that are shed on their pasts bring some shocking and impossible news. Is this relationship doomed? <br /><br />This novel has a paranormal twist with angelic interventions. The locations are descriptive enough to give the reader a realistic picture without interfering with the flow of the story. This could be a matter of preference! The romance is very poignant. Friends' loyalty and support are very well portrayed. The sex scenes are very graphic. The storyline is very well developed and full of suspense and surprises. <br /><br />This would appeal to those who like erotic novels with palpable emotions and endless twists.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3107263409163479288" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Julia Grantham" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36338481-julia-grantham"><img alt="Julia Grantham" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435500677p2/36338481.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2582565093?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julia Grantham" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julia Grantham" href="/user/show/36338481-julia-grantham">Julia Grantham</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2582565093" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11010223298804165621">I loved this book! Brilliant writing <br/><br/>I loved Author C. L. Hunter’s first book in her Soul Mates series and was equally thrilled by this second one, My Soul Belongs to You. It centered on two characters from the first book: Katlyn Reynolds, a successful businesswoman from South Carolina, and Deacon O’Mallery, a top CEO from Dublin.<br/><br/>Sparks erupted from their first contact, but Katlyn and Deacon each had a history of betrayal and abuse that had led them to avoid love and commitment. Could true love </span>
  <span id="freeText11010223298804165621" style="display:none">I loved this book! Brilliant writing <br /><br />I loved Author C. L. Hunter’s first book in her Soul Mates series and was equally thrilled by this second one, My Soul Belongs to You. It centered on two characters from the first book: Katlyn Reynolds, a successful businesswoman from South Carolina, and Deacon O’Mallery, a top CEO from Dublin.<br /><br />Sparks erupted from their first contact, but Katlyn and Deacon each had a history of betrayal and abuse that had led them to avoid love and commitment. Could true love set them free? Suspense and drama unfolded as people from their past chased after them threatening to unravel their hard won emotional equilibrium, not to mention, jeopardize their lives. <br /><br />Hunter’s exquisite writing pulled me in from the start. She has an amazing gift for storytelling that grabs you and doesn’t let go. Her great strength as a writer is her ability to draw the reader into the emotions of her characters. I loved the lush descriptions and use of foreign places, the Irish culture and language that was spot on perfect, never over done, nor making me lose the thread of the drama and love story. Hunter placed me into each scene, so that I could feel, taste, smell and see the sights as they unfolded to the characters, whether in romantic Paris or the raw fisherman’s warehouse, befitting the mind of a deranged man bent on destroying Katlyn and Deacon. <br /><br />The dialogue was witty and smart with a charming use of song lyrics for innuendo and subtle context, fleshing out characters as well as the evolving love affair. As with her first book, Hunter skillfully combined drama, suspense, mystical fantasy, romance and erotica. Yet, the overarching theme was love and commitment. It was a beautiful love story!<br /><br />I am a big C. L. Hunter fan and highly recommend this book. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11010223298804165621" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9338726590092998631">Katlyn Reynolds gave up a daughter for adoption at the tender age of 16 and has since developed a very successful advertisement company while refusing to get close to anyone to protect her heart from further hurt. Then she meets Deacon O'Mallery - a sexy Irish businessman who has put being an orphan with nothing to become second in command of a large intel company. On meeting her he realises Katlyn is his soul-mate and after hearing her story he realises he wants to find his birth mother. Katlyn</span>
  <span id="freeText9338726590092998631" style="display:none">Katlyn Reynolds gave up a daughter for adoption at the tender age of 16 and has since developed a very successful advertisement company while refusing to get close to anyone to protect her heart from further hurt. Then she meets Deacon O'Mallery - a sexy Irish businessman who has put being an orphan with nothing to become second in command of a large intel company. On meeting her he realises Katlyn is his soul-mate and after hearing her story he realises he wants to find his birth mother. Katlyn on the other hand is confused - she feels comfortable enough to share her past but insists he find someone else for a future. Deacon tries desperately to find his birth mother while fighting to make Katlyn realise she has to become his - thankfully he has the spirits Thomas and Calista to help him.<br /><br />This was a lovely story interwoven into a lot of Irish folklore. The agonies that both Katlyn and Deacon were going through were covered quite substantially and I felt that was a little too much as I started to find it boring. However I did enjoy the story and I did like the plot of the story. The writing was clear and easy to understand and feel.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11319428410518594336">My Soul Belongs to You (Soul Mates Book 2) by C.L. Hunter is a well put together combination of genres, not the least of which is romance. Toss in a little touch of angels, eroticism, and huge amounts of charisma and electricity between Katlyn and Deacon and you have a great story. Hunter is great at fully developing the characters and even manages to avoid some of the more common cliches that are so often found in romance novels.   <span id="freeText11319428410518594336" style="display:none">My Soul Belongs to You (Soul Mates Book 2) by C.L. Hunter is a well put together combination of genres, not the least of which is romance. Toss in a little touch of angels, eroticism, and huge amounts of charisma and electricity between Katlyn and Deacon and you have a great story. Hunter is great at fully developing the characters and even manages to avoid some of the more common cliches that are so often found in romance novels. When the two main characters meet, their respective pasts pose some trouble, and could possibly come between them, but Hunter finds a way for true love to prevail. With an added dimension of angels in the spirit world that watch over Katlyn and Deacon, you have a sweet and inspiring element. Thrills and suspense are not far to be found either, and Hunter captures the pace of the plot firmly in this story, guiding the reader to the satisfying ending. Not to be missed for romance lovers and others alike.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11732106537027496816">Although I loved "Your Soul Was Made for Mine" by C.L. Hunter, I believe she excelled herself in every way possible with the marvelous sequel, "My Soul Belongs to You". <br/><br/>This time we are presented with a love story with many ups and downs, like most love stories truly have. I had never enjoyed a romance novel so much since Jane Austen's. This is how good it is.<br/><br/>The settings, the exchange of songs between the lovers, and the overall plot –which sometimes felt like a thriller– made for a must-have f</span>
  <span id="freeText11732106537027496816" style="display:none">Although I loved "Your Soul Was Made for Mine" by C.L. Hunter, I believe she excelled herself in every way possible with the marvelous sequel, "My Soul Belongs to You". <br /><br />This time we are presented with a love story with many ups and downs, like most love stories truly have. I had never enjoyed a romance novel so much since Jane Austen's. This is how good it is.<br /><br />The settings, the exchange of songs between the lovers, and the overall plot –which sometimes felt like a thriller– made for a must-have for all you romance lovers.<br /><br />Although I'm an occasional romance reader –I very much prefer fantasy and science fiction– I have read many romance novels over the years and it felt like ages since I was as moved and excited for a romance novel as I was when reading this one. <br /><br />I was so excited that I read it in one single day! I really recommend it. </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2120671066" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7690656763761519456">Katlyn and Deacon’s story in My Soul Belongs to You is so compelling I forgot this was the second book in the series. Of course after finishing I immediately started on the first, but I don’t feel I missed out on anything from beginning with book two.<br/><br/>Hunter does a fantastic job of developing the characters, and avoiding the predictable clichés we as readers have gotten used to in the overcrowded romance genre. It takes a lot for a book to stand out ahead of its contemporaries and I believe My So</span>
  <span id="freeText7690656763761519456" style="display:none">Katlyn and Deacon’s story in My Soul Belongs to You is so compelling I forgot this was the second book in the series. Of course after finishing I immediately started on the first, but I don’t feel I missed out on anything from beginning with book two.<br /><br />Hunter does a fantastic job of developing the characters, and avoiding the predictable clichés we as readers have gotten used to in the overcrowded romance genre. It takes a lot for a book to stand out ahead of its contemporaries and I believe My Soul Belongs to You absolutely does.<br /><br />The changing backdrop kept me interested while the writing and twists were the real hook. Hunter is a writer I feel will soon be discovered and become a household name, and I’m glad I got to experience her work without any preconceived idea of what I would find.<br /></span>

Reading other reviews of My Soul Belongs to You this is what came across to me so I took the plunge and read it for myself. <br/><br/>C.L.   <span id="freeText16962671835763610941" style="display:none">Series books that also offer enough when reading out of order are a favourite of mine. I discovered this a few years ago by accident, and when going back to start from earlier books there is a whole new realm of depth that further adds to the overall experience. Reading other reviews of My Soul Belongs to You this is what came across to me so I took the plunge and read it for myself. <br /><br />C.L. Hunter is obviously a writer with a lot of talent, which is what first came across to me. I love the characters and how their introduction is handled in such a provocative way. The scene setting is also subtle but painted with just the right amount of detail so that they never overpower the prose, which is fast and punchy. I’m now off to read Your Soul Was Made for Mine, and hoping for further books in the series.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13691719526515198499">I enjoyed "My Soul Belongs to You" by C.L. Hunter. This is the follow up book in the Soul Mates series and I received a complementary copy to read in exchange for an honest review. I was hesitant to continue with this series since the writing is a little formal for my tastes and I'm not usually a big reader in the fantasy/ mystic space, but there was something about the author's writing style that had me so curious to know how the story would continue for these characters. I'm glad I stuck with </span>
  <span id="freeText13691719526515198499" style="display:none">I enjoyed "My Soul Belongs to You" by C.L. Hunter. This is the follow up book in the Soul Mates series and I received a complementary copy to read in exchange for an honest review. I was hesitant to continue with this series since the writing is a little formal for my tastes and I'm not usually a big reader in the fantasy/ mystic space, but there was something about the author's writing style that had me so curious to know how the story would continue for these characters. I'm glad I stuck with it and found myself thoroughly enjoying the path the story takes. I would recommend this to fans of traditional romance novels.<br />Happy Reading...enjoy!</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6795449514686172129">Wow, C L Hunter captures an epic love story in this the second book in her Soul Mates series. The writing is tight and fast and the romance and passion has sparks flying so I didn’t want to stop reading. The backdrop of South Carolina and then Dublin are written with such vivid clarity you feel a part of the story yourself, and if she continues writing this well it’s only a matter of time before Hunter becomes part of the romance big-hitters. A fantastic read, I want more and more.</span>

<div id="review_2150124769" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2150124769" />
    <a title="Book Blast" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast"><img alt="Book Blast" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519305008p2/72437516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2150124769?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Book Blast" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Book Blast" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast">Book Blast</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2150124769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6935034946202254248">Another fantastic read from C L Hunter. My Soul Belongs to You gets underway with the same great writing and fire that I’ve learned to expect, and with Katlyn and Deacon we have great characters that both have complexities and depth. Mystical love affairs don’t come any better than this, believe me, I‘ve read enough of them, and now I can’t wait to read Hunter’s next book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('y+gTKdzYlQQCTni15yIFHO0UcOrdLhpfEz8AkcOecsexP6C/yEVCjQkZJ7B8RaHv/YzvhAFIhc+CW7QlvxGIfw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<script>
//<![CDATA[
      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_35225043'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35225043-western-song?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Western Song<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/5146263.Leigh_Podgorski?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Leigh Podgorski<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.20 avg rating &mdash; 148 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published \n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer10080531301350433649\">When Weston Beaudurant’s buddy, rodeo clown Cody Goode is killed in a rodeo accident -- gored by the maniacal bull Baby Face that Weston is riding, Weston is consumed with guilt. The day after the accident, while going through Cod’s papers, lawyer Wy<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText10080531301350433649\" style=\"display:none\">When Weston Beaudurant’s buddy, rodeo clown Cody Goode is killed in a rodeo accident -- gored by the maniacal bull Baby Face that Weston is riding, Weston is consumed with guilt. The day after the accident, while going through Cod’s papers, lawyer Wynona Vasquez discovers that he had been secretly engaged to a Thai immigrant who is arriving by train that evening.\n	Elected by unanimous decision to be the welcoming committee, Weston arrives at the train station prepared for anything but the lovely forlorn creature he finds waiting in the rain. Though appearing waif-like, Song Phan-Rang is anything but fragile. Her mettle quickly rises to the surface in her determination to remain in Y-oh-ming.\n	Forced together by their circumstances, Weston and Song are explosive. Used to solitude, Weston is driven crazy by the obliging Song. But as Song shows her prowess not only as a housekeeper and cook, but as a rider and rancher as well, Weston discovers that against his best efforts (and damned if he\'ll ever admit it) -- he\'s falling in love.\n	The morning after the Christmas Cotillion, where cowboys by the dozen lined up for a dance with the exotic Song, and Weston wrangled the last one, she discovers her visa has expired. Pledging her Uncle Thieu\'s farm in Thailand as a dowry, Song asks Weston to marry her. Swearing that this is not a good idea at all -- he does.\n	Song blossoms in America. Weston\'s sister Olive, a schoolteacher, helps Song with her English, and introduces her to the ideas of the Founding Fathers, most notably Tom Paine. Firebrand and activist Wynona employs Song in her office. Her first assignment is working with Shoshone shaman MAD BULL and Bull\'s young assistant, Jack Deerstalker as they fight a referendum that would allow gambling on their reservation.\n	As winter melts into spring, Song and Weston continue to profess their marriage is simply one of convenience, though it is obvious to everybody that the two are in love. Obvious to everyone that is, but Jack Deerstalker who has fallen for her himself.\n	One night as Weston returns earlier than expected from a rodeo, he finds Jack in his living room, alone with Song. Enraged, Weston explodes, throwing Jack out of the house. \nThat night a fierce winter storm blows. The creek rises and floods, endangering thirty head of cattle caught on the other side. Song springs into action, riding side by side with Weston. When a baby calf slips into the icy creek, Song plunges in after it. Together, Weston and Song pull the animal free. Weston is knocked speechless by her bravery. Later, as he warms her by a roaring fire, Song and Weston make love for the first time.\n	A few days later, Wynona and Song are introduced to the case of illegal immigrant Thai workers, forced to toil as slaves in the garment industry in El Segundo, California. Song becomes deeply involved with the workers and their plight – the search for a desperate promise of freedom. With her work, she discovers the power true freedom holds.\n	But her work and growing sense of the true power of freedom begins to tear at the budding love between Weston and Song. \nMeanwhile, the referendum Jack, Wynona, and Song fought so hard against has been defeated. There will be no gambling on the reservation. Jack organizes a rodeo to raise money for an investment deal for the reservation. Weston agrees to ride – on one condition. Jack gets the bull, Baby Face that killed Cody.\nThe night before the rodeo, Weston finds a letter Song has written to the garment workers she is helping. “We are, every one of us, entitled to a life with dignity. To life with honor. There are those who would attempt to steal our dignity, to seize our honor. But it is only when we allow this deepest core of our being to be ripped from us that we become enslaved. Remember, you, too, have been touched by God.”\nThe next morning, Weston leaves for the rodeo without her. \nAt the rodeo, in an eerie replay of Cody’s accident, the bull throws Weston. Song nurses Weston back to health, but still torn between freedom\'s power and her growing love, Song knows she must ultimately choose. \nSeveral weeks later, with Weston well on his way to mending, Song and Olive host a dinner party at Snowy Moon to celebrate Weston’s recovery. Along with Zeb, Jack Deerstalker and Mad Bull are there to join in the festivities. But in the middle of the revelry, the phone rings: it’s Jenny Chang and it’s about the case of the immigrant workers.\nSong knows she must go.\nThe next day, Weston drives her to the train station.\nReturning to the ranch, Weston, still suffering from his injuries, limps painfully to the corral, and saddles up his horse. He rides across the rolling plains to the waterfall where he and Song had spent so much time in happier times now long gone by. Watching the water tumble by like his lost hope, suddenly, Weston picks up a stone, and fires it into the tumultuous fall. He whistles for his horse, and throws himself into the saddle.\nAcross the plains, the train continues to roll. Inside, an uproar arises among the passengers. Song forces her way to the window.\n Outside, riding like hell, is Weston.\nSong’s heart begins to pound.\nAnd suddenly, she knows….Finally, she knows.\nSong grabs her suitcase, and elbows her way through the crowd.\nBefore the train fully stops, she is bounding from the platform…and rushing into Weston’s arms.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"10080531301350433649\" href=\"#\" The author is from the Maasai, a pastoralist community who have been able to maintain their culture and traditions despite the pressure exerted on their lifestyle by modernization. He gives a detailed account of the struggle experienced by his culture\'s gradual transformation in order to conform to the new world order. Traditionally, it was considered sunrise was the beginning of a day, yet in this formal world, a day begins at midnight and ends at the same time. Snyder did when he joined it;• German atrocities toward captured crew and civilians;• behind-the-scenes stories of the Belgium civilians who risked all to save American flyers who were in the air one moment, spiraling down in flames the next;• creation and dedication of the monument to the Susan Ruth and its crew located in Macquenoise, Belgium in 1989.Shot Down was created from the vast number of letters and journals of Howard Snyder; diaries of men and women on the ground who rescued, sheltered and hid the crew; and interviews conducted by historians. Centered around the 306th Bomb Group in Thurleigh, England, it is informative, insightful and captivating.For most, 70 years is a long time ago. World War II fades in importance as each year goes by. Shot Down moves history out of the footnotes into reality, keeping the stories of real people alive as they experience being shot down. You are there, almost holding your breath as Lt.
